|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1250">所有傳輸規則新增到郵件中的收件者人數上限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1250">Maximum number of recipients added to a message by all transport rules</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1251">100 位收件者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1251">100 recipients</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1252">100 位收件者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1252">100 recipients</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1253">100 位收件者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1253">100 recipients</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1254">100 位收件者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1254">100 recipients</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1255">100 位收件者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1255">100 recipients</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1256">100 位收件者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1256">100 recipients</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1285">收件匣規則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1285">Inbox rule</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1286">256kb<sup>1</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1286">256kb<sup>1</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1287">256kb<sup>1</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1287">256kb<sup>1</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1288">256kb<sup>1</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1288">256kb<sup>1</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1289">256kb<sup>1</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1289">256kb<sup>1</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1290">256kb<sup>1</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1290">256kb<sup>1</sup></span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1291">256kb<sup>1</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1291">256kb<sup>1</sup></span></span>|

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1292"><sup>1</sup> 如果信箱已遷移至 Exchange Online，則可能會將收件匣規則限制設定為低於預設 EXO 值的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1292"><sup>1</sup> If a mailbox was migrated to Exchange Online, the inbox rule limit might be set to the value that is lower than the default EXO value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1293">如果是這種情況，可以增加收件匣規則值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1293">If that is the case, the inbox rule value can be increased.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1294">如需相關指示，請參閱[修改 Exchange Online 中收件匣規則使用的空間](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/clients-and-mobile-in-exchange-online/outlook-on-the-web/increase-the-space-used-by-inbox-rules)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1294">For instructions, see [Modify the space used by Inbox rules in Exchange Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/exchange/clients-and-mobile-in-exchange-online/outlook-on-the-web/increase-the-space-used-by-inbox-rules).</span></span> 

### <a name="journal-transport-and-inbox-rule-limits-across-standalone-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1295">不同獨立選項的日誌、傳輸和收件匣規則限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1295">Journal, transport, and inbox rule limits across standalone options</span></span>

## <a name="moderation-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1341">仲裁限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1341">Moderation limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1342">這些限制會控制在通訊群組和傳輸規則套用之郵件核准所採用的仲裁設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1342">These limits control the moderation settings that are used for message approval applied to distribution groups and transport rules.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1343">**仲裁信箱的大小上限**：如果仲裁信箱超過此限制，需要仲裁的郵件會就包含在傳回給寄件者的未傳遞回報 (NDR) 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1343">**Maximum size of the arbitration mailbox**: If the arbitration mailbox exceeds this limit, messages that require moderation are returned to the sender in a non-delivery report (NDR).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1344">**仲裁者人數上限**：可指派給單一仲裁通訊群組的仲裁者人數上限，或是可使用單一傳輸規則新增到郵件中的仲裁者人數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1344">**Maximum number of moderators**: The maximum number of moderators that you can assign to a single moderated distribution group or that can be added to a message using a single transport rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1345">請注意，您無法將通訊群組指定為仲裁者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1345">Note that you can't specify a distribution group as a moderator.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1346">**等候仲裁之郵件的到期日**：根據預設，等候仲裁的郵件會在兩天後過期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1346">**Expiration for messages waiting for moderation**: By default, a message waiting for moderation expires after two days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1347">不過，過期的仲裁郵件處理會每七天執行一次，</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1347">However, the processing of expired moderated messages runs every seven days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1348">也就是說，仲裁郵件會在兩天到九天之間的任何時候過期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1348">This means that a moderated message can expire at any time between two and nine days.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1349">**過期仲裁通知郵件的最大速率**：這項限制會設定過期仲裁郵件一小時內的通知郵件數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1349">**Maximum rate for expired moderation notification messages**: This limit sets the maximum number of notification messages for expired moderated messages in a one-hour period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1350">這項限制是設置在資料中心內的每個信箱資料庫上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1350">This limit is placed on each mailbox database in the datacenter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-p192">在大量使用期間，某些寄件者可能不會收到有關仲裁郵件已過期的通知郵件。不過，這些通知還是可以使用傳遞回報找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-p192">During periods of heavy usage, some senders may not receive notification messages for moderated messages that have expired. However, these notifications are still discoverable using delivery reports.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-p193"><sup>1</sup> 這是 Exchange Server 2013 組織的預設限制。系統管理員可以為其組織變更此值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-p193"><sup>1</sup> This is the default limit for Exchange Server 2013 organizations. ## <a name="exchange-activesync-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1417">Exchange ActiveSync 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1417">Exchange ActiveSync limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1418">下列限制適用於 Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync，這是一種用戶端通訊協定，可以同步處理行動裝置與 Exchange 之間的信箱資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1418">The following limits apply to Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync, a client protocol that synchronizes mailbox data between mobile devices and Exchange.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1419">**Exchange ActiveSync 裝置限制**：每個信箱的 Exchange ActiveSync 裝置數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1419">**Exchange ActiveSync device limit**: The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices per mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="a2aad-1420">**Exchange ActiveSync 裝置刪除限制**：Exchange 系統管理員可以在一個月內刪除的 Exchange ActiveSync 裝置數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a2aad-1420">**Exchange ActiveSync device deletion limit**: The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices that an Exchange administrator can delete in a single month.</span></span>
